    "from IPython.html.widgets import interact, fixed\n",
    "\n",
    "def add(x, y, absolute=False):\n",
    "    if absolute:\n",
    "        return abs(x) + abs(y)\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        return x + y\n",
    "\n",
    "def show_add(x, y, absolute=False):\n",
    "    print \"The sum is\", add(x, y, absolute)\n",
    "\n",
    "#show_add(3,10)\n",

    "def sinewave(freq=1.0):\n",
    "    x = np.linspace(0., 360., 91, endpoint=True)  # Generate uniformly spaced 1-d array\n",
    "    y = np.sin(freq*x*np.pi/180.)                      # Compute sin(x)\n",
    "    pylab.plot(x, y, \"--r\", linewidth=2.5)\n",
    "\n",
    "    pylab.xlim(0, 360.)      # Set X-axis limits\n",
    "    pylab.ylim(-1.5, 1.5)    # Set Y-axis limits\n",
    "\n",
    "interact(sinewave, freq=(0.0, 4.0))"

   "source": [
    "import netCDF4\n",
    "import mpl_toolkits.basemap as bm\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n",
    "%pylab inline\n",
    "\n",
    "def tempheight(month):    \n",
    "\n",
    "    ncf = netCDF4.Dataset(\"air.mon.ltm.nc\", \"r\")\n",
    "    ncf2 = netCDF4.Dataset(\"hgt.mon.ltm.nc\", \"r\")\n",
    "    lat_data = ncf.variables[\"lat\"][14:27]\n",
    "    lon_data = ncf.variables[\"lon\"][92:121]\n",
    "\n",
    "    temp_data = ncf.variables[\"air\"][month-1,0,14:27,92:121]\n",
    "    hgt_data = ncf2.variables[\"hgt\"][month-1,5,14:27,92:121]\n",
    "    ncf.close()\n",
    "    ncf2.close()\n",
    "\n",
    "    mapproj = bm.Basemap(projection= 'cyl',llcrnrlat=25.0, llcrnrlon=230,urcrnrlat=55.0, urcrnrlon=300)\n",
    "    mapproj.drawcoastlines()\n",
    "    mapproj.drawcountries()\n",
    "    mapproj.drawstates()\n",
    "    mapproj.drawparallels(np.array([30, 40, 50]), labels=[1,0,0,0])\n",
    "    mapproj.drawmeridians(np.array([-120, -100, -80]), labels=[0,0,0,1])\n",
    "    mymapf = pylab.contourf(lon_data, lat_data, temp_data, 10,cmap=pylab.cm.jet)\n",
    "    mymap = pylab.contour(lon_data, lat_data, hgt_data, 10,colors='k')  \n",
    "    pylab.colorbar(mymapf, orientation='horizontal')\n",
    "    pylab.title(\"Month \"+str(month))\n",
    "    return pylab.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "tempheight(1)"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "import mpl_toolkits.basemap as bm\n",
    "\n",
    "import netCDF4\n",
    "\n",
    "def us_plot(month):\n",
    "\n",
    "    ncf = netCDF4.Dataset(\"air.mon.ltm.nc\", \"r\")\n",
    "    lon = ncf.variables[\"lon\"][:]\n",
    "    lat = ncf.variables[\"lat\"][:]\n",
    "    temp_data = ncf.variables[\"air\"][month-1,0,:,:]\n",
    "\n",
    "    mapproj = bm.Basemap(projection='lcc', lat_0=30, lon_0=250,\n",
    "                     llcrnrlat=20.0, llcrnrlon=230,\n",
    "                     urcrnrlat=55.0, urcrnrlon=310)\n",
    "    mapproj.drawcoastlines()\n",
    "    lonall, latall = np.meshgrid(lon, lat)\n",
    "    lonproj, latproj = mapproj(lonall, latall)\n",
    "    pylab.contourf(lonproj, latproj, temp_data, 20)\n",
    "    pylab.colorbar()\n",
    "    pylab.title(\"Month \"+str(month))\n",
    "\n",
    "interact(us_plot, month=(1,12))"
   ]
  },

    "## Using ``pandas`` in the notebook\n",
    "\n",
    "``pandas`` is a powerful data analysis package for spreadsheet-like operations in Python.\n",
    "\n",
    "We will work through a simple example from *Wes McKinney's* book *Python for Data Analysis* using IPython Notebook,\n",
    "which provides a nicer-lokking display of ``pandas`` output.\n",
    "\n",
    "First, install ``pandas``:\n",
    "\n",
    "    conda install pandas\n",
    "\n",
    "From the Social Security Administration website http://www.ssa.gov/oact/babynames/limits.html\n",
    "download the National Data for popular baby names in the U.S. in the file ``naames.zip``\n",
    "\n",
    "Create sub-folder named ``names`` in the folder where your notebook is running.\n",
    "Unzip the downloaded file in the ``names`` sub-folder (this create a large number of files)\n",
    "\n"
